Day: <<print $day>>\n\n<<silently>>\n<<set $daysremaining = 10 - $day>>\n<<set $intelligence = $intelligence + 5>>\n<<set $happiness = $happiness - 2>>\n<<set $social_life = $social_life + 5>>\n<<endsilently>>\n\n<<if $intelligence lte -10>>Your cub is dangerously dumb. WVU might not even accept him.<<endif>><<if $intelligence gte -9 and $intelligence lte -5>>Your cub likes walking into walls and tumbling around.<<endif>><<if $intelligence gte -4 and $intelligence lte 0>>Your cub is rather dull.<<endif>><<if $intelligence gte 1 and $intelligence lte 5>>Your cub is curious, analyzing the world around him<<endif>><<if $intelligence gte 6 and $intelligence lte 10>> Your cub is sharp, quickly learning new things <<endif>><<if $intelligence gte 11 and $intelligence lte 15>> Your cub is street smart, able to think on his feet<<endif>><<if $intelligence gte 16 and $intelligence lte 20>> Your cub is smart, processing information much faster than the average cub<<endif>><<if $intelligence gte 21 and $intelligence lte 25>> Your cub is wise, pondering the philosophical nuances of society<<endif>><<if $intelligence gte 26>> Your cub is a genius. Harvard here we come! <<endif>>\n<<if $happiness gte -9 and $happiness lte -5>>And he's close to running away, might want to be careful<<endif>><<if $happiness gte -4 and $happiness lte 0>>And he's moping around.<<endif>><<if $happiness gte 1 and $happiness lte 5>>And he might crack a smile once in a while<<endif>><<if $happiness gte 6 and $happiness lte 10>> And he's occasionally happy <<endif>><<if $happiness gte 11 and $happiness lte 15>> And he's relatively happy!<<endif>><<if $happiness gte 16 and $happiness lte 20>> And he's pretty happy!<<endif>><<if $happiness gte 21 and $happiness lte 25>> And he's super happy!<<endif>><<if $happiness gte 26>> And he's ridiculously happy! <<endif>><<if $social_life lte - 10>> But great news: He's socially exiled!<<endif>>\n<<if $social_life gte -9 and $social_life lte -5>>But fortunately he's socially oppressed<<endif>><<if $social_life gte -4 and $social_life lte 0>>But fortunately he doesn't have anyone to talk to<<endif>><<if $social_life gte 1 and $social_life lte 5>>But he has a good friend that he likes to talk to<<endif>><<if $social_life gte 6 and $social_life lte 10>> But why is he so social??? <<endif>><<if $social_life gte 11 and $social_life lte 15>> He has three friends. This is getting outrageous<<endif>><<if $social_life gte 16 and $social_life lte 20>> But he has WAY too many friends<<endif>><<if $social_life gte 21 and $social_life lte 25>> What are you even doing? He has WAY too many friends<<endif>><<if $social_life gte 26>> Your cub's dreams of Harvard have been replaced by ideas of friendship and socializing<<endif>>\n\n<<if $happiness lte -10>> Your cub became so unhappy he ran away. Can't raise a cub if he ain't there! Harvard here we come! <<endif>>\n<<if $happiness gte -9 and $happiness lte -5>>And he's close to running away, might want to be careful<<endif>><<if $happiness gte -4 and $happiness lte 0>>And he's moping around.<<endif>><<if $happiness gte 1 and $happiness lte 5>>And he might crack a smile once in a while<<endif>><<if $happiness gte 6 and $happiness lte 10>> And he's occasionally happy <<endif>><<if $happiness gte 11 and $happiness lte 15>> And he's relatively happy!<<endif>><<if $happiness gte 16 and $happiness lte 20>> And he's pretty happy!<<endif>><<if $happiness gte 21 and $happiness lte 25>> And he's super happy!<<endif>><<if $happiness gte 26>> And he's ridiculously happy! <<endif>><<if $social_life lte - 10>> But great news: He's socially exiled!<<endif>>\n<<if $social_life gte -9 and $social_life lte -5>>But fortunately he's socially oppressed<<endif>><<if $social_life gte -4 and $social_life lte 0>>But fortunately he doesn't have anyone to talk to<<endif>><<if $social_life gte 1 and $social_life lte 5>>But he has a good friend that he likes to talk to<<endif>><<if $social_life gte 6 and $social_life lte 10>> But why is he so social??? <<endif>><<if $social_life gte 11 and $social_life lte 15>> He has three friends. This is getting outrageous<<endif>><<if $social_life gte 16 and $social_life lte 20>> But he has WAY too many friends<<endif>><<if $social_life gte 21 and $social_life lte 25>> What are you even doing? He has WAY too many friends<<endif>><<if $social_life gte 26>> Your cub's dreams of Harvard have been replaced by ideas of friendship and socializing<<endif>>\n\n<<if $happiness lte -10>> Your cub became so unhappy he ran away. Can't raise a cub if he ain't there! [[Game over|endScreen]] :( \n\n<<else>>It's currently day <<print $day>>. You have <<print $daysremaining>> more days left until the end of your parenthood. You are a tiger mom. Tiger moms make sure their cubs are as intelligent as possible, no matter what. Happiness is a bonus but it is much less important than intelligence. However, if your cubs happiness dips too low he might run away. Social life is never important; in fact, keep that as low as possible. You have 10 days to get your cub into Harvard, good luck. \n\n[[return to main page|Start]]
